 congress ke sutron ne bataaya ki party kii sarvocch samiti ek prastaav paarit kar adhyaksh sonia gandhi ko raashtrapati pad ke liye apane ummidavaar kaa chayan karne ke liye adhikrut kar sakati he
 Sources said that the situation arising out of the recent increase in petrol prices and the problems facing the party in Andhra Pradesh are also likely to be discussed
 vistaarit congress kaarysmiti kii baithak main pradhanmantri manmohan singh or varisht mantriyon ke alaava party ke mukhyamantriyon, pradesh adhyakshon, vishesh rup se aamantrit sadasyon tathaa sthaayee aamantriton ke bhaag lene kii sambhaavna he
 The meeting is going to take place exactly one day after the joint demonstrations by yoga guru Baba Ramdev and Team Anna against corruption
 team anna ne koyala blokon ke aavanton main aniyamittaaon ke liye pradhanmantri ko jimmedaar tehraate hue isaki nishpaksh jaanch kii maang kii he
 The Congress Working Committee meeting is also expected to discuss the party's performance in the assembly elections held in five states earlier this year and the party's preparations for the assembly elections in Himachal Pradesh and Gujarat a few months later
 gauratlab he ki chunaav main party ke pradarshan kaa vishleshan karne ke liye congress adhyaksh sonia gandhi ne raksha mantri eke antni kii adhyakshata main ek samiti kaa gathan kiya tha
 This committee has submitted its report
 congress ke sutron ne bataaya ki baithak main raashtrapati pad ke liye party ke ummidavaar ke chayan ke silsile main ghatak dalon se ab tak hui baatcheet par charchaa kii jaaegi
 The party will announce its candidate after the notification is issued
 raashtrapati chunaav ke liye adhisuchana june ke madhya tak jari hone kii sambhaavna he
 Names of Finance Minister Pranab Mukherjee and Vice President Hamid Ansari are among the potential Congress candidates, but the party is yet to express its choice
 yah bhi pataa chalaa he ki party ke kuch logon ne pradhanmantri manmohan singh kaa naam raashtrapati pad ke liye prastaavit kiya he, lekin ek varisht netaa ne kaha ki aisa hone kii sambhaavna nahin he
 The comments congress ke sutron ne bataaya ki party ke ummidavaar kii ghoshnaa se pehle ghatak dalon ke saath vichaar-vimarsh kiye jane kii sambhaavna he
 It is noteworthy that President Pratibha Patil's term is going to end in July this year

 yah baithak bhrashtachar ke khilaaf yoga guru baba ramdev or team anna dwaara sanyukt rup se kiye gaye pradarshnon ke thik ek din baad hone ja rahi he
 Team Anna has demanded a fair inquiry into the allocation of coal blocks, holding the Prime Minister responsible for the irregularities
 congress kaarysmiti kii baithak main is varsh kii shuruyaat main paanch rajyon main hue vidhansabha chunaav main party ke pradarshan tathaa kuch maheenon baad himachal pradesh or gujarat main hone vaale vidhansabha chunaav ke liye party kii taiyaariyon par charchaa hone kii bhi sambhaavna he
 Significantly, Congress President Sonia Gandhi had formed a committee under the chairmanship of Defense Minister AK Antony to analyze the performance of the party in the elections
 yah samiti apni report saunp chuki he
 Sources in the Congress said that the meeting so far will be discussed with the constituents in connection with the selection of the party's candidate for the presidency
 party adhisuchana jari hone ke baad apane ummidavaar kii ghoshnaa karegi

 Here is the talk of Kailash Kher's upcoming album Ishq Anokha
 kailash kher ke band 'kailasa' ke is album ke gaanon puure ho chuke hai or kaha ja rahaa he ki yah album kaaphi ruhani or rahasypurna he

 kailash kherke geet mere liye hameshaa se khaas rahe hai

 Hundreds of people took part in peace processions and prayer meetings in Kansas for Srinivas Kuchibhotla, an Indian engineer killed in racial violence in America
 samachar patr consaas city star ke mutabik, pichley saptaah ghrinaaspad aparaadh main ghayal hue bhartiya naagarik alok madsaani ne ravivaar ko oleth ke ball conference centre main yojit shanti juluus tathaa prarthana sabha main hissaa liya
 The prayer meeting was organized by the India Association of Kansas City
 madsaani ne kaha, "kaash! vah ek sapana hota
 " ullekhneey he ki consaas ke oleth main austins baar and greel main ek purv america nausainik adam dablyoo parinton ne goli markar ejeeniyar kuchibhotla (32) kii hatya kar di thi or alok reddy madsaani (32) ko ghayal kar diya tha
 Ian Grillot (24), an American citizen who came to the rescue in the case, was also injured, who is currently in hospital

 "kuchibhotla and Madasani used to work at electronic manufacturing company Garmin
